I've got this idea brewing in my mind, and I couldn't wait to share it with you all! üéâ I've started a GitHub repository where we can collaborate on solving the GeeksforGeeks Daily Practice of Coding Problems of the Day (POTD) in C++.

I believe it could be a fantastic opportunity for us to come together, share our solutions, and learn from each other's approaches. Plus, it's a chance to enhance our problem-solving skills while having fun!

Would any of you be interested in joining me on this coding adventure? It doesn't matter if you're a seasoned pro or just starting out; all skill levels are welcome! üîó Repository Link: [https://github.com/mrpankajpandey/GFG-POTD24]

üéØ Why Contribute?

Sharpen your problem-solving skills by tackling diverse challenges.
Learn from others' solutions and different approaches.
Build a portfolio of your coding solutions on GitHub.
Contribute to the learning journey of fellow programmers.
üí° How to Contribute?

1. Fork the repository.
2. Clone the forked repository to your local machine.
3. Add your solutions in C++ to the appropriate directory.
4. Follow the contribution guidelines outlined in the README.md.
5. Submit a Pull Request with a clear description of your changes.
ü§ù Join Us!
Whether you're a seasoned coder or just starting your coding journey, there's room for everyone to contribute and learn together. Let's make this repository a valuable resource for the programming community!

Spread the word, invite your friends, and let's embark on this coding adventure together!

08:11:38 Ishu üáÆüá≥: You are given a 2D matrix grid of size 3 x 3 consisting only of characters 'B' and 'W'. Character 'W' represents the white color, and character 'B' represents the black color.

Your task is to change the color of at most one cell so that the matrix has a 2 x 2 square where all cells are of the same color.
Return true if it is possible to create a 2 x 2 square of the same color, otherwise, return false
08:12:45 Revanth: I solved in java using brute force
08:13:00 Ishu üáÆüá≥: Input: grid = [["B","W","B"],["B","W","W"],["B","W","B"]]

Output: true

Explanation:

It can be done by changing the color of the grid[0][2]
08:13:09 Ishu üáÆüá≥: here is one testcase
08:13:27 Ishu üáÆüá≥: how i solve this
08:13:52 Ishu üáÆüá≥: what is the flowchart or algo to solve
08:15:27 Revanth: There are four 2x2 matrices and count each w frequency and b frequency for each 2x2 matrix.
If for any matrix w==1 or b==1 or w==4 or b==4
Return true
Otherwise false
08:39:38 Mohammed Aqib: Just traverse entire grid and check condition just keep in mind loops will terminate 1 step early as you will compare (i,j) , (i+1,j) , (i,j+1) , (i+1,j+1). So if 3 of these 4 have same value for any 2X2 matrix return 1 and if entire loop terminates without returning 1 then return 0

11:06:51 Amit Kumar Yadav: c++ solution class Solution {
public:
// Function to sort the given doubly linked list using Merge Sort.
struct Node *sortDoubly(struct Node *head) {
if(head == NULL)
return head;
Node *temp = head;
vector arr;
while(temp != nullptr){
arr.push_back(temp->data);
temp = temp->next;
}
sort(arr.begin(), arr.end());
struct Node *newNode = new Node(arr[0]);
struct Node *dummyHead = newNode;
for(int i = 1; i < arr.size(); i++){
Node *temp_node = new Node(arr[i]);
dummyHead->next = temp_node;
temp_node->prev = dummyHead;
dummyHead = temp_node;
}
return newNode;
}
};

As a MLSA you will be featured on their website. Along with this you will be a part of the global . community of MLSA Along with this you will receive
For alpha:
1) free subscription for Microsoft technology
2) 7-8 redeem code for most Microsoft software
3) LinkedIn premium+ free LinkedIn learning

If you achieve beta then:
1)beta swagkit that includes (tshirt,cube,stickers,bottle,stressball and more)
2) MLSA ID card
3) certificate
4) MVP Badge


Last milestone is GOLD:
1)You will receive 1-1 mentorship from. Microsoft official
2) gold swag kit( Table lamp, Headphones, Laptop sleeve and more)
3) gold MLSA badge
4) specially featured on their website

09:55:06 Aman Sir Gfg Interview: POLL:
Are you aware of Mongodb? What is the functionality of the same
OPTION: Yes (36 votes)
OPTION: No (20 votes)
09:55:48 Kstij: for database using Nosql
09:57:06 Aman Sir Gfg Interview: Okay!
More answers
10:02:38 Deepak Yadav: It is a NoSQL and open source database which is used for storing large scale of data
10:03:11 Ujjwal Mishra: To store structured and unstructured data. Mainly in json format.
10:03:48 pulkit: Stores data in schemaless form. In memory level it stores in BSON format
10:04:48 Saksham Jain: It is a nosql database, providing easy integration with various technologies, it uses BSON which is similar to JSON which makes it easy to use with javascript apps
10:15:46 Kamya Mehra: Basically a nosql db
10:42:23 SR: It is used mostly to handle large crowd or load who interact with the servers in large scale..
11:00:55 Aman Sir Gfg Interview: Why should someone use MongoDB and not MySql
11:04:56 ~Bharath: Mongo db is mostly used in web applications due to real time analysis and stores unstructured data whereas Mysql stores only structured data in relational database.
11:05:05 Malay Jain Modi: it generally depends on our project

if we are working on a real time data which evolves frequently and the data is unstructured
then mongo DB is good

other wise for a structured abd relational data base MySQL

I use MySQL so i don't know much about mongo db
11:05:17 Sai Shankar: Mongodb is horizontally scalable
11:05:55 SR: There are a lot of constraints in MySql that are not suitable for server which aims scalability..and MongoDB gives those flexibilities like for example in one collection we can use multiple data types but in sql its not possible and in sql we have to follow ACID properties but in MongoDB these constraints are not there..and there many other advantages..
11:08:00 Aman Sir Gfg Interview: 24 people said that they know about mongodb.
Atleast more than half should write something
11:14:02 Mukilan üíô: Mongo is faster and flexible..but MySQL is slower because it organise the information in tables. For higher speed mongo is better choice.. and it is beginner friendly to learn..

09:03:51 Krishna Jadhav: int solve(int currnum,vector&store,int n){
if(currnum == n){
return 0;
}
if(currnum > n){
return INT_MAX;
}
if(store[currnum]!=-1){
return store[currnum];
}
int afteradd = solve(currnum + 1,store,n);
if(currnum == 0){
store[currnum] = afteradd+1;
return store[currnum];
}
int afterdouble = solve(2*currnum,store,n);
store[currnum] = min(afteradd,afterdouble)+1;
return store[currnum];
}
int minOperation(int n)
{
int currnum = 0;
vectorstore(n,-1);
return solve(currnum,store,n);
}

11:04:02 Aditya Gaur: Certainly, here's a sample project proposal for an Attendance Portal Website:

---

# Project Proposal: Attendance Portal Website

## Introduction

The Attendance Portal Website project aims to create a comprehensive and user-friendly platform for managing attendance records in an educational institution. This web-based system will serve various user roles, including administrators, faculty members, students, the Dean, and Heads of Departments (HODs). The system will allow for efficient attendance recording, data management, and communication between different stakeholders.

## Project Objectives

The primary objectives of this project are as follows:

1. **Automated Attendance Management:** Develop an automated attendance tracking system to streamline the process of recording and managing attendance for students.

2. **User-Friendly Interface:** Create an intuitive web interface for easy login, attendance tracking, and data retrieval by various users.

3. **Role-Based Access Control:** Implement role-based access control to ensure that only authorized users can perform specific actions within the system.

4. **Data Security:** Prioritize the security of sensitive data, including personal information, attendance records, and user credentials.

5. **Efficient Communication:** Enable efficient communication between faculty, students, and administrative personnel for attendance-related matters.

6. **Notification System:** Implement a notification system to keep users informed about updates, notices, and important events.

## Project Components

The project will consist of the following key components:

### 1. 0-Level Data Flow Diagram (DFD)
- An overview of the system and its main stakeholders.

### 2. User Roles
- Administrator, Dean, HODs, Faculty, and Students, each with specific permissions and actions.

### 3. Administrative Portal
- Allows administrators to manage user accounts, handle requests, and monitor system operations.

### 4. HOD Portal
- Enables HODs to manage faculty, assign subjects, and view departmental attendance data.

### 5. Faculty Portal
- Allows faculty to take attendance, view assigned subjects, and communicate with students.

### 6. Dean Portal
- Provides access to Deans for viewing all assigned subjects, managing attendance, and personal information.

### 7. Student Portal
- Enables students to view attendance data, subject information, and receive notifications.

### 8. Database Management
- Backend databases for storing user data, attendance records, and communication data.

### 9. Notification System
- An integrated notification system for sending and receiving important updates.

## Methodology

We will follow the Agile project management methodology to ensure flexibility, collaboration, and iterative development. Regular meetings and feedback sessions with stakeholders will be held to incorporate changes and updates as needed.

## Timeline

The project will be divided into phases, each with its deliverables and timelines:

- Phase 1: Requirement Analysis and System Design (Month 1-2)
- Phase 2: Development and Testing (Month 3-6)
- Phase 3: User Training and Pilot Testing (Month 7-8)
- Phase 4: Deployment and Maintenance (Month 9 onwards)

## Budget

The estimated budget for this project includes costs for development, testing, hardware, software licenses, and maintenance. A detailed budget breakdown will be provided in the project plan.

## Conclusion

The Attendance Portal Website project is a crucial system for the efficient management of attendance records in our educational institution. We believe that by implementing this system, we will improve data accuracy, enhance communication, and simplify administrative tasks related to attendance. We look forward to your approval and support for the successful execution of this project.

If you have any questions or require further information, please do not hesitate to contact us.

---

This project proposal outlines the objectives, components, methodology, timeline, and budget for the Attendance Portal Website project. Adjustments can be made based on specific requirements and expectations.

08:49:15 Naresh M: I will share my opinion, most of the people are trying to learn new trending tech stacks, but let me tell you that will not a good option for you now, why? See learning these tech stacks doesn't require any special background knowledge and any one can learn it, and as a fresher when joining a company literally no product based company questions you on tech stacks, so just drop that idea unless you want to get into service based jobs and get underpaid,

focus on only two things now as a CS student,

1. DSA
2. learn core subjects (CN, C programming, Digital Logic, DBMS, OS, CD, TOC)
This will be make you interview ready when you get into your final year, you don't need tech stacks and if you wonder what about projects that is secondary, you can do them in the last 2 or 3 months when you are ready
